Coupled with warm and fun service, hustle and bustle of the busy outlet as well as alive and fun ambiance, Sailendra offers its guests an experience to be remembered. Sailendra serves a large variety of local and international favorites. The buffet is a popular choice and always a sell-out item at the restaurant. Wood-fired pizza is something to look out for, while a wide variety of authentic local dishes are also available, including dishes such as sop buntut, mie ayam (chicken noodle), chicken rice, laksa, and nasi goreng (fried rice). For those who prefer to stay seated and do with less walking, an enticing a la carte is also available. All dishes, both buffet and a la carte, are prepared with the best quality produce and presented in a fun yet modern style.
